DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Avoid interactive prompts and update base
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          software-properties-common \
          apt-transport-https \
          ca-certificates \
          lsb-release && \
      # Add PPA for GCC 13 if required
      add-apt-repository -y ppa:ubuntu-toolchain-r/test && \
      apt-get update && \
      # Core development tools
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          g++-13 \
          build-essential \
          cmake \
          meson \
          ninja-build \
          make \
          git \
          curl \
          wget \
          pkg-config \
          python3 \
          python3-pip \
          python3-setuptools \
          python3-wheel \
          clang-format \
          abigail-tools \
          docker-compose-plugin \
          libssl-dev \
          openssl \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbrotli-dev \
          libzstd-dev \
          libcurl4-openssl-dev \
          netcat-openbsd \
          libgtest-dev \
          squid \
          # Useful utilities
          tzdata && \
      # Set GCC/G++ 13 as default
      update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-13 120 && \
      update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 120 && \
      # Upgrade pip
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip && \
      # Install/Upgrade meson (if newer needed) and pre-commit via pip
      python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade meson pre-commit && \
      # Clean up
      apt-get clean && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/yhirose_cpp-httplib
  # Ensure /usr/local/bin is in PATH and python points to python3
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3 /usr/bin/python
  # (Optionally) Verify toolchain versions
  RUN g++ --version && \
      cmake --version && \
      meson --version && \
      ninja --version && \
      clang-format --version && \
      abidiff --version && \
      python3 --version && \
      openssl version && \
      pre-commit --version
  # (Optional) Expose default ports for testing, e.g., 8080
  # EXPOSE 8080
  # Default command: bash shell
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 120
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Install/Upgrade meson (if newer needed) and pre-commit via pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade meson pre-commit
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/yhirose_cpp-httplib
  # Ensure /usr/local/bin is in PATH and python points to python3
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3 /usr/bin/python
  # (Optionally) Verify toolchain versions
  RUN g++ --version && \
      cmake --version && \
      meson --version && \
      ninja --version && \
      clang-format --version && \
      abidiff --version && \
      python3 --version && \
      openssl version && \
      pre-commit --version

      update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 120
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Install/Upgrade meson (if newer needed) and pre-commit via pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade meson pre-commit
  # Set working directory

  # Ensure /usr/local/bin is in PATH and python points to python3
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3 /usr/bin/python
  # (Optionally) Verify toolchain versions
  RUN g++ --version && \
      cmake --version && \
      meson --version && \
      ninja --version && \

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Avoid interactive prompts and update base
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          software-properties-common \
          apt-transport-https \
          ca-certificates \
          lsb-release \
          gnupg \
          dirmngr && \
      apt-get clean && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Add PPA in a separate step, handle potential Release file changes
  RUN apt-get update --allow-releaseinfo-change && \
      add-apt-repository -y ppa:ubuntu-toolchain-r/test && \
      apt-get update
  # Separate installation of g++-13 and toolchain for easier debugging
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          g++-13 \
          build-essential \
          -o Debug::pkgProblemResolver=yes && \
      apt-get clean && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install remaining build and runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \

  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-13 120 && \
      update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 120
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Install/Upgrade meson (if newer needed) and pre-commit via pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade meson pre-commit
  # Set working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/yhirose_cpp-httplib
  # Ensure /usr/local/bin is in PATH and python points to python3
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/bin:${PATH}"

      cmake --version && \
      meson --version && \
      ninja --version && \

  # EXPOSE 8080

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          software-properties-common \
          apt-transport-https \
          ca-certificates \
          lsb-release \
          gnupg \
          dirmngr && \
      apt-get clean && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN apt-get update --allow-releaseinfo-change && \
      add-apt-repository -y ppa:ubuntu-toolchain-r/test && \
      apt-get update
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          g++-13 \
          build-essential \
          -o Debug::pkgProblemResolver=yes && \
      apt-get clean && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Split apt-get install for easier debugging and to isolate potential problematic packages
  # Core build tools and Python
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          cmake \
          meson \
          ninja-build \
          make \
          git \
          curl \
          wget \
          pkg-config \
          python3 \
          python3-pip \
          python3-wheel \
          clang-format && \
      apt-get clean && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Remaining libraries/utilities (excluding problematic packages for Ubuntu 22.04)
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          libssl-dev \
          openssl \
          zlib1g-dev \
          libbrotli-dev \
          libzstd-dev \
          libcurl4-openssl-dev \
          netcat-openbsd \
          libgtest-dev \
          squid \
          tzdata && \
      apt-get clean && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install setuptools via pip (since python3-setuptools package name may cause issues)
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade setuptools
  # Set GCC/G++ 13 as default
  RUN update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/gcc gcc /usr/bin/gcc-13 120 && \
      update-alternatives --install /usr/bin/g++ g++ /usr/bin/g++-13 120
  # Upgrade pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip
  # Install/Upgrade meson (if newer needed) and pre-commit via pip
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --upgrade meson pre-commit
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/yhirose_cpp-httplib
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3 /usr/bin/python
  RUN g++ --version && \
      cmake --version && \
      meson --version && \
      ninja --version && \
      clang-format --version && \
      python3 --version && \
      openssl version && \
      pre-commit --version
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
